<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="English">English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=child&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: English">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=child&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Alternative forms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/childe#English" title="childe">childe</a></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=child&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/child#Middle_English" title="child">child</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/cild#Old_English" title="cild">ċild</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href="/wiki/fetus" title="fetus">fetus</a>; <a href="/wiki/female" title="female">female</a> <a href="/wiki/baby" title="baby">baby</a>; child</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/kel%C3%BEaz" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/kelþaz">*kelþaz</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href="/wiki/womb" title="womb">womb</a>; <a href="/wiki/fetus" title="fetus">fetus</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/g(%27)elt-&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/g(')elt- (page does not exist)">*g(')elt-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href="/wiki/womb" title="womb">womb</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href="/wiki/kuld#Danish" title="kuld">kuld</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href="/wiki/brood" title="brood">brood</a>, <a href="/wiki/litter" title="litter">litter</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv"><a href="/wiki/kull#Swedish" title="kull">kull</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href="/wiki/brood" title="brood">brood</a>, <a href="/wiki/litter" title="litter">litter</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is"><a href="/wiki/kelta#Icelandic" title="kelta">kelta</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="is"><a href="/wiki/kjalta#Icelandic" title="kjalta">kjalta</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href="/wiki/lap" title="lap">lap</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%F0%90%8C%BA%F0%90%8C%B9%F0%90%8C%BB%F0%90%8C%B8%F0%90%8C%B4%F0%90%8C%B9&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="𐌺𐌹𐌻𐌸𐌴𐌹 (page does not exist)">𐌺𐌹𐌻𐌸𐌴𐌹</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn"><a href="/w/index.php?title=kil%C3%BEei&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="kilþei (page does not exist)">kilþei</a></span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href="/wiki/womb" title="womb">womb</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E0%A4%9C%E0%A4%B0%E0%A5%8D%E0%A4%A4&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="जर्त (page does not exist)">जर्त</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jarta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa"><a href="/wiki/%E0%A4%9C%E0%A4%B0%E0%A5%8D%E0%A4%A4%E0%A5%81#Sanskrit" title="जर्तु">जर्तु</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jártu</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href="/wiki/vulva" <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=child&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">child</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en plural-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/children#English" title="children">children</a></b> <i>or</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">dialectal or archaic</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en plural-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/childer#English" title="childer">childer</a></b>)</p>
<ol>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/person" title="person">person</a> who has not <a href="/wiki/yet" title="yet">yet</a> <a href="/wiki/reach" title="reach">reached</a> <a href="/wiki/adulthood" title="adulthood">adulthood</a>, whether <a href="/wiki/natural" title="natural">natural</a> (<a href="/wiki/puberty" title="puberty">puberty</a>), <a href="/wiki/cultural" title="cultural">cultural</a> (<a href="/wiki/initiation" title="initiation">initiation</a>), or <a href="/wiki/legal" title="legal">legal</a> (<a href="/wiki/majority" title="majority">majority</a>)
<dl>
<dd>
<div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Go easy on him: he is but a <b>child</b>.</i></div>
</dd>
</dl>
</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#obsolete" title="Appendix:Glossary">obsolete</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> specifically</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a <a href="/wiki/female" title="female">female</a> child, a <a href="/wiki/girl" title="girl">girl</a>.
<span class="HQToggle"><a>quotations ▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;">
<li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Shakespeare">Shakespeare</a>
<dl>
<dd>A boy or a <b>child</b>, I wonder?</dd>
</dl>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">with possessive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/one" title="one">One</a>'s <a href="/wiki/son" title="son">son</a> or <a href="/wiki/daughter" title="daughter">daughter</a>, <a href="/wiki/regardless" title="regardless">regardless</a> of <a href="/wiki/age" title="age">age</a>.
<dl>
<dd>
<div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">My youngest <b>child</b> is forty-three.</i></div>
</dd>
</dl>
</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/cartomancy" title="cartomancy">cartomancy</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The thirteenth <a href="/wiki/Lenormand" title="Lenormand">Lenormand</a> card.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#figurative" title="Appendix:Glossary">figuratively</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href="/wiki/figurative" title="figurative">figurative</a> <a href="/wiki/offspring" title="offspring">offspring</a>, <i><a href="/wiki/particularly" title="particularly">particularly</a>:</i>
<ol>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/person" title="person">person</a> <a href="/wiki/considered" title="considered">considered</a> a <a href="/wiki/product" title="product">product</a> of a <a href="/wiki/place" title="place">place</a> or <a href="/wiki/culture" title="culture">culture</a>, a <a href="/wiki/member" title="member">member</a> of a <a href="/wiki/tribe" title="tribe">tribe</a> or <a href="/wiki/culture" title="culture">culture</a>, <a href="/wiki/regardless" title="regardless">regardless</a> of <a href="/wiki/age" title="age">age</a>.
<span class="HQToggle"><a>quotations ▼</a></span><dl>
<dd>
<div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The <b>children</b> of Israel.</i></div>
</dd>
<dd>
<div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">He is a <b>child</b> of his times.</i></div>
</dd>
</dl>
<ul style="display: none;">
<li><b>1984</b>, Mary Jane Matz, <i>The Many Lives of Otto Kahn: A Biography</i>, page 5:
<dl>
<dd>For more than forty years, he preached the creed of art and beauty. He was heir to the ancient wisdom of Israel, a <b>child</b> of Germany, a subject of Great Britain, later an American citizen, but in truth a citizen of the world.</dd>
</dl>
</li>
<li><b>2009</b>, Edward John Moreton Dunsany, <i>Tales of Wonder</i>, page 64:
<dl>
<dd>Plash-Goo was of the <b>children</b> of the giants, whose sire was Uph. And the lineage of Uph had dwindled in bulk for the last five hundred years, till the giants were now no more than fifteen foot high; but Uph ate elephants <span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span></dd>
</dl>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/anything" title="anything">Anything</a> <a href="/wiki/derive" title="derive">derived</a> from or <a href="/wiki/caused" title="caused">caused</a> by <a href="/wiki/something" title="something">something</a>.
<span class="HQToggle"><a>quotations ▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;">
<li><b>1991</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Salman_Rushdie" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Salman Rushdie">Salman Rushdie</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Midnight%27s_%27%27%27Children%27%27%27" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Midnight's '''Children'''">Midnight's <b>Children</b></a></i></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dd>
<div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Poverty, disease, and despair are the <b>children</b> of war.</i></div>
</dd>
</dl>
<ul style="display: none;">
<li>
<div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2013</b> June 7,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joseph_Stiglitz" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Joseph Stiglitz">Joseph Stiglitz</a>,  “<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/commentisfree/2013/may/27/globalisation-is-about-taxes-too">Globalisation is about taxes too</a>”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Guardian_Weekly" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Guardian Weekly">The Guardian Weekly</a></cite>, volume 188, number 26, page 19:</span>
<dl>
<dd><span class="cited-passage">It is time the international community faced the reality: we have an unmanageable, unfair, distortionary global tax regime. […] It is the starving of the public sector which has been pivotal in America no longer being the land of opportunity – with a <b>child'</b>s life prospects more dependent on the income and education of its parents than in other advanced countries.</span></dd>
</dl>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/computing" title="computing">computing</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href="/wiki/data" title="data">data</a> <a href="/wiki/item" title="item">item</a>, <a href="/wiki/process" title="process">process</a>, or <a href="/wiki/object" title="object">object</a> which has a <a href="/wiki/subservient" title="subservient">subservient</a> or <a href="/wiki/derivative" title="derivative">derivative</a> <a href="/wiki/role" title="role">role</a> <a href="/wiki/relative" title="relative">relative</a> to <a href="/wiki/another" title="another">another</a>.
<span class="HQToggle"><a>quotations ▼</a></span><dl>
<dd>
<div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The <b>child</b> node then stores the actual data of the parent node.</i></div>
</dd>
</dl>
<ul style="display: none;">
<li><b>2011</b>, John Mongan, Noah Kindler, Eric Giguère, <i>Programming Interviews Exposed</i>
<dl>
<dd>The algorithm pops the stack to obtain a new current node when there are no more <b>children</b> (when it reaches a leaf).</dd>
</dl>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>

<input type="text" size="4" name="nclass1" title="The noun class of the word in the singular or citation form." /> Plural class: <input type="text" size="4" name="nclass2" title="The noun class of the word in the plural form, if any." /></p><span style="display: none;"><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:Transliteration">Transliteration</a>: <input name="tr" title="The word transliterated into the Latin alphabet." /> (e.g. ázbuka for азбука)</span><p style="display: none;">Raw page name: <input name="rawPageName" title="The word without all of the dictionary-only diacritics." /> (e.g. amo for amō)</p><p style="display: none;">Qualifier: <input name="qual" title="A qualifier for the word" /> (e.g. literally, formally, slang)</p><p style="display: block;"><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:List_of_scripts">Script code</a>: <input name="sc" size="6" title="The script code to apply to this word." />(e.g. Cyrl for Cyrillic, Latn for Latin)<br /></p><p style="display: <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Middle_English">Middle English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=child&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Middle English">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms_2">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=child&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Alternative forms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/chyld#Middle_English" title="chyld">chyld</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/chylde#Middle_English" title="chylde">chylde</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/childe#Middle_English" title="childe">childe</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/chelde#Middle_English" title="chelde">chelde</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/cild#Middle_English" title="cild">cild</a></span></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=child&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/cild#Old_English" title="cild">ċild</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/kel%C3%BEaz" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/kelþaz">*kelþaz</a></i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_2">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=child&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English_phonology" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Middle English phonology">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/ˈtʃiːld/</span></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=child&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="enm">child</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b><span class="Latn" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/children#Middle_English" title="children">children</a></span></b> or <b><span class="Latn" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/childre#Middle_English" title="childre">childre</a></span></b>)</p>
<ol>
<li><a href="/wiki/baby" title="baby">baby</a>, <a href="/wiki/infant" title="infant">infant</a>, <a href="/wiki/toddler" title="toddler">toddler</a></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/child#English" title="child">child</a></span>, <a href="/wiki/kid" title="kid">kid</a></li>
<li>An <a href="/wiki/offspring" title="offspring">offspring</a>, one of one's <a href="/wiki/progeny" title="progeny">progeny</a>.</li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/childish" title="childish">childish</a> or <a href="/wiki/stupid" title="stupid">stupid</a> <a href="/wiki/individual" title="individual">individual</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Chrisitanity</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the <a href="/wiki/Christ_child" title="Christ child">Christ child</a>; <a href="/wiki/Jesus" title="Jesus">Jesus</a> as a <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/child#English" title="child">child</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#figurative" title="Appendix:Glossary">figuratively</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A member of a creed <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">usually with the religion in the genitive preposing it</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>A young male, especially one employed as an <a href="/wiki/hireling" title="hireling">hireling</a>.</li>
<li>A young noble training to become a knight; a <a href="/wiki/squire" title="squire">squire</a> or <a href="/wiki/childe" title="childe">childe</a>.</li>
<li>The young of <a href="/wiki/animals" title="animals">animals</a> or <a href="/wiki/plants" title="plants">plants</a>.</li>
<li>A material as a <a href="/wiki/result" title="result">result</a> or <a href="/wiki/outcome" title="outcome">outcome</a>.</li>
</ol>
